about_this_resource_text: '<p>Prof. Szolovits covers Natural Language Processing methods
  including those which are not based on neural networks representations and those
  techniques which employ neural network architectures.</p> <p>Speaker: Peter Szolovits</p>             <p><a
  href="./resolveuid/d39a6eed387ee90b1f72a01949c35c7b">Lecture 8:&nbsp;Natural Language
  Processing (NLP), Part 2 slides (PDF - 2.0MB)</a></p>'

  <span m="539930">patterns</span> <span m="540650">and</span> <span m="540860">thesaurus</span>
  <span m="541490">terms.</span> <span m="541890">So</span> <span m="542150">we</span>
  <span m="542330">looked</span> <span m="542690">up,</span> <span m="543350">in</span>
  <span m="543500">the</span> <span m="543800">UMLS,</span> <span m="545390">words</span>
  <span m="545840">and</span> <span m="545960">phrases</span> <span m="546650">to</span>
  <span m="546800">see</span> <span m="547070">if</span> <span m="547220">they</span>
  <span m="547430">matched</span> <span m="547820">some</span> <span m="548120">clinically</span>
  <span m="548630">meaningful</span> <span m="549170">term.</span> <span m="550580">We</span>
  <span m="550790">had</span> <span m="551000">patterns</span> <span m="551720">that</span>
  <span m="551930">identified</span> <span m="552680">things</span> <span m="553010">like</span>
  <span m="554180">phone</span> <span m="554510">numbers</span> <span m="555050">and</span>
  <span m="555170">social</span> <span m="555500">security</span> <span m="556040">numbers</span>
  <span m="556610">and</span> <span m="556730">addresses</span> <span m="557390">and</span>
  <span m="557510">so</span> <span m="557780">on.</span></p><p><span m="559140">And</span>
  <span m="559220">then</span> <span m="559700">we</span> <span m="559940">did</span>
  <span m="560920">parsing</span> <span m="561710">of</span> <span m="561890">the</span>
  <span m="562010">text.</span> <span m="562620">So</span> <span m="563240">in</span>
  <span m="563390">those</span> <span m="563650">days,</span> <span m="563960">we</span>

  <span m="565790">Parser,</span> <span m="567480">which,</span> <span m="567740">doesn't</span>
  <span m="568070">make</span> <span m="568310">a</span> <span m="568370">whole</span>
  <span m="568520">lot</span> <span m="568760">of</span> <span m="568850">difference</span>
  <span m="569300">what</span> <span m="569530">parser.</span> <span m="570470">But</span>
  <span m="570740">you</span> <span m="570860">get</span> <span m="571100">either</span>
  <span m="571400">a</span> <span m="571490">constituent</span> <span m="572480">or</span>
  <span m="572960">constituency</span> <span m="573860">or</span> <span m="574070">dependency</span>

  <span m="576320">you</span> <span m="576500">relationships</span> <span m="577670">among</span>
  <span m="578030">the</span> <span m="578150">words.</span> <span m="579420">And</span>
  <span m="579530">so</span> <span m="579950">it</span> <span m="580100">allows</span>
  <span m="580610">you</span> <span m="581360">to</span> <span m="582380">include,</span>
  <span m="583010">as</span> <span m="583280">features,</span> <span m="584300">the</span>
  <span m="584450">way</span> <span m="584780">in</span> <span m="584960">which</span>
  <span m="585620">a</span> <span m="585770">word</span> <span m="586130">that</span>
  <span m="586400">you're</span> <span m="586550">looking</span> <span m="586940">at</span>

  <span m="588170">words</span> <span m="588620">around</span> <span m="589040">it.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="598460">all</span> <span m="598730">of</span> <span m="598880">the</span>
  <span m="599000">words</span> <span m="599540">that</span> <span m="599750">are</span>

  <span m="604430">original</span> <span m="604940">word</span> <span m="605270">that</span>
  <span m="605510">you're</span> <span m="605630">focusing</span> <span m="606320">on,</span>
  <span m="607040">or</span> <span m="607310">that</span> <span m="607520">are</span>
  <span m="607700">linked</span> <span m="608420">by</span> <span m="608810">within</span>

  <span m="814150">typical</span> <span m="814750">way</span> <span m="815470">for</span>

  <span m="1984070">rules</span> <span m="1984910">that</span> <span m="1985180">say</span>

  <span m="1987160">terms</span> <span m="1987640">in</span> <span m="1987760">the</span>
  <span m="1987850">language</span> <span m="1988360">correspond</span> <span m="1989080">to</span>
  <span m="1989230">certain</span> <span m="1989650">concepts</span> <span m="1990970">and</span>
  <span m="1991210">that</span> <span m="1991420">they</span> <span m="1991600">are</span>
  <span m="1991720">a</span> <span m="1991780">combinatorially,</span> <span m="1993790">functionally</span>
  <span m="1994540">combined</span> <span m="1995380">as</span> <span m="1995680">the</span>
  <span m="1995800">syntax</span> <span m="1996430">directs,</span> <span m="1997420">in</span>
  <span m="1997600">order</span> <span m="1997870">to</span> <span m="1998020">give</span>
  <span m="1998290">us</span> <span m="1998530">a</span> <span m="1998710">semantic</span>
  <span m="1999280">representation.</span></p><p><span m="2000870">So</span> <span
  m="2001050">we</span> <span m="2001200">don't</span> <span m="2001440">know</span>
  <span m="2001650">how</span> <span m="2001830">to</span> <span m="2001950">do</span>
  <span m="2002160">either</span> <span m="2002430">of</span> <span m="2002550">those</span>
  <span m="2002850">very</span> <span m="2003120">well.</span> <span m="2004090">And</span>
  <span m="2004200">so</span> <span m="2004440">the</span> <span m="2004560">current,</span>
  <span m="2005200">the</span> <span m="2005340">contemporary</span> <span m="2006180">idea</span>
  <span m="2006810">about</span> <span m="2007140">language</span> <span m="2007590">modeling</span>
  <span m="2008670">is</span> <span m="2008880">to</span> <span m="2009000">say,</span>
  <span m="2010200">given</span> <span m="2010620">a</span> <span m="2010680">sequence</span>

  <span m="2019980">language</span> <span m="2020430">model.</span> <span m="2021480">So</span>
  <span m="2021630">obviously,</span> <span m="2022200">you</span> <span m="2022350">can't</span>

  <span m="2278070">it.</span> <span m="2278190">But</span> <span m="2278370">anyway,</span>

  <span m="2279480">corpus.</span> <span m="2280890">And</span> <span m="2281100">they</span>
  <span m="2281310">said--</span> <span m="2282330">so</span> <span m="2282570">Shakespeare</span>

  <span m="2568320">trigrams,</span> <span m="2569040">&quot;They</span> <span m="2569280">also</span>

  nine</span> <span m="2570600">point</span> <span m="2571050">six</span> <span m="2571500">billion</span>
  <span m="2571890">from</span> <span m="2573090">two hundred</span> <span m="2573555">four</span>
  <span m="2574020">oh</span> <span m="2574420">six</span> <span m="2574820">three</span>
  <span m="2575220">percent</span> <span m="2575610">of</span> <span m="2576000">the</span>
  <span m="2576120">rates</span> <span m="2576510">of</span> <span m="2576630">interest</span>
  <span m="2576990">stores</span> <span m="2577980">as</span> <span m="2578160">Mexico</span>
  <span m="2578820">and</span> <span m="2578980">Brazil.&quot;</span> <span m="2580050">So</span>
  <span m="2580830">you</span> <span m="2580980">could</span> <span m="2581160">imagine</span>
  <span m="2581700">that</span> <span m="2581880">this</span> <span m="2582120">is</span>
  <span m="2582240">some</span> <span m="2582510"><i>Wall</i></span> <span m="2582720"><i>Street</i></span>
  <span m="2583200"><i>Journal</i></span> <span m="2583620">writer</span> <span m="2584190">on</span>
  <span m="2584400">acid</span> <span m="2587940">writing</span> <span m="2588360">this</span>
  <span m="2588600">text.</span> <span m="2589080">Because</span> <span m="2589830">it</span>
  <span m="2589950">has</span> <span m="2590340">a</span> <span m="2590430">little</span>
  <span m="2590670">bit</span> <span m="2590880">of</span> <span m="2591030">the</span>
  <span m="2591120">right</span> <span m="2591390">kind</span> <span m="2591630">of</span>
  <span m="2591690">flavor.</span></p><p><span m="2593850">So</span> <span m="2594240">more</span>
  <span m="2594510">recently,</span> <span m="2596040">people</span> <span m="2596430">said,</span>

  <span m="2598350">to</span> <span m="2598500">make</span> <span m="2598800">use</span>
  <span m="2599160">of</span> <span m="2599310">this</span> <span m="2599850">in</span>
  <span m="2600180">some</span> <span m="2601440">systematic</span> <span m="2602220">way</span>
  <span m="2602520">to</span> <span m="2602700">help</span> <span m="2603030">us</span>
  <span m="2603240">with</span> <span m="2603510">our</span> <span m="2603630">language</span>
  <span m="2604050">analysis</span> <span m="2604650">tasks.</span> <span m="2605730">So</span>
  <span m="2606870">to</span> <span m="2607080">me,</span> <span m="2607410">the</span>

  <span m="2610590">this</span> <span m="2610800">direction</span> <span m="2611790">was</span>

  <span m="2613390">Mikolov's</span> <span m="2614760">approach</span> <span m="2615240">to</span>
  <span m="2615390">doing</span> <span m="2615720">this.</span> <span m="2616440">And</span>
  <span m="2616680">he</span> <span m="2616860">developed</span> <span m="2617340">two</span>
  <span m="2617580">models.</span></p><p><span m="2618540">He</span> <span m="2618660">said,</span>

  <span m="2626580">to</span> <span m="2626730">use</span> <span m="2627420">is</span>
  <span m="2627690">co-occurrence</span> <span m="2628800">data</span> <span m="2629910">on</span>
  <span m="2631774">a</span> <span m="2632550">series</span> <span m="2633150">of</span>
  <span m="2633300">tokens</span> <span m="2634170">in</span> <span m="2634350">the</span>

  <span m="2635220">trying</span> <span m="2635520">to</span> <span m="2635640">model.</span>
  <span m="2636840">And</span> <span m="2637050">we're</span> <span m="2637230">going</span>
  <span m="2637560">to</span> <span m="2638010">use</span> <span m="2638400">a</span>
  <span m="2638490">neural</span> <span m="2638820">network</span> <span m="2639300">model</span>

  <span m="2641730">word</span> <span m="2642600">from</span> <span m="2643020">the</span>
  <span m="2643140">words</span> <span m="2643560">around</span> <span m="2643980">it.</span>

  <span m="2656670">word.</span></p><p><span m="2659590">And</span> <span m="2659970">so</span>
  <span m="2660150">what</span> <span m="2660390">we're</span> <span m="2660540">going</span>
  <span m="2660810">to</span> <span m="2660930">find</span> <span m="2661590">is</span>
  <span m="2661830">that</span> <span m="2662490">words</span> <span m="2662970">that</span>
  <span m="2663150">tend</span> <span m="2663480">to</span> <span m="2663750">appear</span>

  <span m="2845570">see</span> <span m="2846440">is</span> <span m="2846710">that</span>

  <span m="3143370">based</span> <span m="3143910">on</span> <span m="3145860">an</span>

  <span m="3147390">trying</span> <span m="3147750">to</span> <span m="3147870">do</span>
  <span m="3148110">this.</span> <span m="3148920">And</span> <span m="3149160">SEDFE</span>
  <span m="3150300">is</span> <span m="3150570">the</span> <span m="3150690">technique</span>
  <span m="3151260">that</span> <span m="3151440">I've</span> <span m="3151590">just</span>
  <span m="3151830">described.</span> <span m="3153000">And</span> <span m="3153270">what</span>
  <span m="3153510">you</span> <span m="3153630">see</span> <span m="3153900">is</span>
  <span m="3154110">that</span> <span m="3155270">the</span> <span m="3155730">automatic</span>
  <span m="3156360">techniques</span> <span m="3157410">for</span> <span m="3157800">many</span>
  <span m="3158190">of</span> <span m="3158340">these</span> <span m="3159180">phenotypes</span>
  <span m="3160410">are</span> <span m="3160560">just</span> <span m="3160890">about</span>
  <span m="3161220">as</span> <span m="3161370">good</span> <span m="3162000">as</span>
  <span m="3162300">the</span> <span m="3162810">manually</span> <span m="3163350">curated</span>
  <span m="3163920">ones.</span> <span m="3164760">And</span> <span m="3164940">of</span>
  <span m="3165030">course,</span> <span m="3165330">they</span> <span m="3165480">require</span>
  <span m="3165990">much</span> <span m="3166290">less</span> <span m="3166560">manual</span>
  <span m="3166980">curation.</span> <span m="3167640">Because</span> <span m="3168510">they're</span>
  <span m="3168690">using</span> <span m="3169140">this</span> <span m="3169350">automatic</span>
  <span m="3169890">learning</span> <span m="3170250">approach.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="3182700">a</span> <span m="3182760">new</span> <span m="3183030">de-identifier</span>
  <span m="3185040">that</span> <span m="3185280">has</span> <span m="3185580">this</span>
  <span m="3185820">rather</span> <span m="3186150">complicated</span> <span m="3186900">architecture.</span>

  <span m="3192810">recursive</span> <span m="3193380">neural</span> <span m="3193680">network</span>
  <span m="3194160">model</span> <span m="3195720">that</span> <span m="3196500">is</span>
  <span m="3197190">implemented</span> <span m="3198330">over</span> <span m="3198690">the</span>
  <span m="3198840">character</span> <span m="3199440">sequences</span> <span m="3200490">of</span>
  <span m="3200700">words</span> <span m="3201390">in</span> <span m="3201600">the</span>
  <span m="3201810">medical</span> <span m="3202260">text.</span> <span m="3203280">So</span>
  <span m="3203970">why</span> <span m="3204240">character</span> <span m="3204750">sequences?</span>

  <span m="3206670">be</span> <span m="3206820">important?</span></p><p><span m="3213140">Well,</span>
  <span m="3213620">consider</span> <span m="3214190">a</span> <span m="3214250">misspelled</span>

  <span m="3460620">2018</span> <span m="3461370">has</span> <span m="3461580">been</span>

  <span m="3465480">or</span> <span m="3465690">more</span> <span m="3465930">accurately,</span>

  <span m="3686420">attention</span> <span m="3686960">to?</span> <span m="3687320">And</span>

  <span m="3704180">order</span> <span m="3704480">to</span> <span m="3704900">produce</span>
  <span m="3705350">the</span> <span m="3705500">output.</span></p><p><span m="3706880">Now,</span>
  <span m="3708870">a</span> <span m="3709010">classical</span> <span m="3709640">linguist</span>
  <span m="3710390">would</span> <span m="3710630">look</span> <span m="3710870">at</span>

  <span m="3728240">But</span> <span m="3728450">from</span> <span m="3728720">an</span>
  <span m="3728810">engineering</span> <span m="3729380">point</span> <span m="3729680">of</span>
  <span m="3729740">view,</span> <span m="3730270">it</span> <span m="3730430">works</span>
  <span m="3730820">quite</span> <span m="3731120">well.</span></p><p><span m="3732990">So</span>
  <span m="3733550">then</span> <span m="3733820">for</span> <span m="3734060">a</span>
  <span m="3734120">while,</span> <span m="3734450">that</span> <span m="3734690">was</span>

  <span m="3735470">the</span> <span m="3735620">art.</span> <span m="3736700">And</span>
  <span m="3736850">then</span> <span m="3737030">last</span> <span m="3737420">year,</span>

  <span m="3742940">along</span> <span m="3743450">and</span> <span m="3743630">said,</span>

  <span m="4017650">degree</span> <span m="4018190">to</span> <span m="4018400">which</span>
  <span m="4019210">the</span> <span m="4019420">encoding</span> <span m="4020260">of</span>
  <span m="4020560">the</span> <span m="4020740">word</span> <span m="4021100">&quot;it&quot;</span>
  <span m="4021850">depends</span> <span m="4022540">on</span> <span m="4022870">the</span>
  <span m="4023140">other</span> <span m="4023380">words</span> <span m="4023830">in</span>
  <span m="4023980">the</span> <span m="4024100">sentence.</span> <span m="4025300">And</span>
  <span m="4025480">you</span> <span m="4025630">see</span> <span m="4025930">that</span>
  <span m="4026140">it's</span> <span m="4026350">focused</span> <span m="4027010">on</span>
  <span m="4027250">the</span> <span m="4027460">animal,</span> <span m="4028900">which</span>
  <span m="4029140">makes</span> <span m="4029380">sense.</span> <span m="4029860">Because</span>
  <span m="4030280">&quot;it,&quot;</span> <span m="4030700">in</span> <span m="4030850">fact,</span>
  <span m="4031270">is</span> <span m="4031450">referring</span> <span m="4034215">to</span>
  <span m="4034480">the</span> <span m="4034660">animal</span> <span m="4035370">in</span>
  <span m="4035530">this</span> <span m="4035660">sentence.</span></p><p><span m="4037210">Here</span>
  <span m="4037600">they</span> <span m="4037810">introduce</span> <span m="4038950">another</span>
  <span m="4039730">encoding.</span> <span m="4041020">And</span> <span m="4041230">this</span>
  <span m="4041500">one</span> <span m="4041740">focuses</span> <span m="4042730">on</span>
  <span m="4043030">&quot;was</span> <span m="4043360">too</span> <span m="4043540">tired,&quot;</span>
  <span m="4045160">which</span> <span m="4045400">is</span> <span m="4045550">also</span>
  <span m="4045910">good.</span> <span m="4046210">Because</span> <span m="4046690">&quot;it,&quot;</span>
  <span m="4047050">again,</span> <span m="4047600">refers</span> <span m="4048610">to</span>
  <span m="4049150">the</span> <span m="4049330">thing</span> <span m="4049630">that</span>
  <span m="4049810">was</span> <span m="4050080">too</span> <span m="4050260">tired.</span>
  <span m="4052490">And</span> <span m="4052640">of</span> <span m="4052760">course,</span>
  <span m="4053270">by</span> <span m="4053510">multi-headed,</span> <span m="4054350">they</span>
  <span m="4054560">mean</span> <span m="4054890">that</span> <span m="4055100">it's</span>
  <span m="4055520">doing</span> <span m="4055910">this</span> <span m="4056150">many</span>
  <span m="4056450">times.</span> <span m="4057440">And</span> <span m="4057620">so</span>
  <span m="4057860">you're</span> <span m="4058280">identifying</span> <span m="4059600">all</span>
  <span m="4059750">kinds</span> <span m="4060200">of</span> <span m="4060350">different</span>
  <span m="4060740">relationships</span> <span m="4062940">in</span> <span m="4063350">the</span>
  <span m="4063500">input</span> <span m="4063830">sentence.</span></p><p><span m="4065930">Well,</span>
  <span m="4066440">along</span> <span m="4066800">the</span> <span m="4066890">same</span>
  <span m="4067250">lines</span> <span m="4068780">is</span> <span m="4069050">this</span>
  <span m="4070520">encoding</span> <span m="4071060">called</span> <span m="4071450">ELMo.</span>
  <span m="4072380">People</span> <span m="4072710">seem</span> <span m="4072980">to</span>
  <span m="4073130">like</span> <span m="4074120"><i>Sesame</i></span> <span m="4074600"><i>Street</i></span>
  <span m="4074900">characters.</span> <span m="4076970">So</span> <span m="4077330">ELMo</span>
  <span m="4077720">is</span> <span m="4077900">based</span> <span m="4078230">on</span>
  <span m="4078380">a</span> <span m="4078440">bi-directional</span> <span m="4079280">LSTM.</span>
  <span m="4080090">So</span> <span m="4080360">it's</span> <span m="4080540">an</span>
  <span m="4080660">older</span> <span m="4080990">technology.</span></p><p><span
  m="4082670">But</span> <span m="4082880">what</span> <span m="4083120">it</span>
  <span m="4083180">does</span> <span m="4083600">is,</span> <span m="4083870">unlike</span>
  <span m="4084350">Word2Vec,</span> <span m="4086200">which</span> <span m="4086500">built</span>
  <span m="4089320">an</span> <span m="4089650">embedding</span> <span m="4090190">for</span>
  <span m="4090550">each</span> <span m="4090820">type--</span> <span m="4092000">so</span>
  <span m="4092350">every</span> <span m="4092620">time</span> <span m="4092950">the</span>
  <span m="4093070">word</span> <span m="4095050">&quot;junk&quot;</span> <span m="4095710">appears,</span>
  <span m="4097060">it</span> <span m="4097300">gets</span> <span m="4097630">the</span>
  <span m="4097720">same</span> <span m="4098080">embedding.</span> <span m="4099229">Here</span>
  <span m="4099760">what</span> <span m="4099970">they're</span> <span m="4100149">saying</span>
  <span m="4100689">is,</span> <span m="4101029">hey,</span> <span m="4101330">take</span>
  <span m="4101529">context</span> <span m="4102130">seriously.</span> <span m="4103510">And</span>
  <span m="4103689">we're</span> <span m="4103840">going</span> <span m="4104140">to</span>
  <span m="4104260">calculate</span> <span m="4104950">a</span> <span m="4105040">different</span>
  <span m="4105520">embedding</span> <span m="4106540">for</span> <span m="4106870">each</span>
  <span m="4107170">occurrence</span> <span m="4108430">in</span> <span m="4108609">context</span>
  <span m="4110050">of</span> <span m="4110229">a</span> <span m="4110290">token.</span></p><p><span
  m="4112710">And</span> <span m="4112830">this</span> <span m="4113069">turns</span>
  <span m="4113370">out</span> <span m="4113550">to</span> <span m="4113670">be</span>
  <span m="4113850">very</span> <span m="4114120">good.</span> <span m="4114899">Because</span>
  <span m="4115439">it</span> <span m="4115620">goes</span> <span m="4115950">part</span>
  <span m="4116279">of</span> <span m="4116399">the</span> <span m="4116490">way</span>
  <span m="4116760">to</span> <span m="4116939">solving</span> <span m="4118200">the</span>
  <span m="4118950">word-sense</span> <span m="4119550">disambiguation</span> <span

  <span m="4121890">is</span> <span m="4122069">just</span> <span m="4122310">an</span>
  <span m="4122430">example.</span> <span m="4123580">If</span> <span m="4123660">you</span>
  <span m="4123810">look</span> <span m="4124050">at</span> <span m="4124170">the</span>
  <span m="4124319">word</span> <span m="4124590">&quot;play&quot;</span> <span m="4125729">in</span>
  <span m="4126029">GloVe,</span> <span m="4126600">which</span> <span m="4126899">is</span>
  <span m="4127050">a</span> <span m="4127109">slightly</span> <span m="4127620">more</span>

  <span m="4129479">the</span> <span m="4129569">Word2Vec</span> <span m="4130290">approach,</span>
  <span m="4131640">you</span> <span m="4131819">get</span> <span m="4132120">playing,</span>
  <span m="4132569">game,</span> <span m="4132960">games,</span> <span m="4133410">played,</span>
  <span m="4133740">players,</span> <span m="4134250">plays,</span> <span m="4134670">player,</span>
  <span m="4135870">play,</span> <span m="4136170">football,</span> <span m="4136680">multiplayer.</span>
  <span m="4137520">This</span> <span m="4137819">all</span> <span m="4138029">seems</span>
  <span m="4138420">to</span> <span m="4138540">be</span> <span m="4138720">about</span>
  <span m="4139020">games.</span> <span m="4140390">Because</span> <span m="4140609">probably,</span>
  <span m="4141479">from</span> <span m="4141810">the</span> <span m="4142140">literature</span>
  <span m="4142740">that</span> <span m="4142950">they</span> <span m="4143100">got</span>
  <span m="4143340">this</span> <span m="4143550">from,</span> <span m="4144300">that's</span>

  <span m="4146430">word</span> <span m="4147210">&quot;play.&quot;</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4160080">ability</span> <span m="4160979">to</span> <span m="4161130">hit</span>

  <span m="4162550">his</span> <span m="4162689">all-around</span> <span m="4163229">excellent</span>
  <span m="4163680">play.&quot;</span> <span m="4164609">So</span> <span m="4164819">this</span>

  <span m="4166290">baseball</span> <span m="4166770">player.</span> <span m="4167970">And</span>
  <span m="4168210">here</span> <span m="4168510">is,</span> <span m="4168660">&quot;They</span>
  <span m="4168779">were</span> <span m="4168960">actors</span> <span m="4169470">who</span>
  <span m="4169620">had</span> <span m="4169740">been</span> <span m="4170279">handed</span>

  <span m="4171479">a</span> <span m="4171540">successful</span> <span m="4172229">play.&quot;</span>
  <span m="4173100">So</span> <span m="4173279">this</span> <span m="4173520">is</span>
  <span m="4173670">a</span> <span m="4173729">different</span> <span m="4174120">meaning</span>

  <span m="4174960">play.</span> <span m="4175979">And</span> <span m="4176130">so</span>
  <span m="4176370">this</span> <span m="4176670">embedding</span> <span m="4177750">also</span>
  <span m="4178229">has</span> <span m="4178500">made</span> <span m="4179040">really</span>
  <span m="4179399">important</span> <span m="4180540">contributions</span> <span

  <span m="4182790">quality</span> <span m="4183240">of</span> <span m="4183330">natural</span>
  <span m="4183689">language</span> <span m="4184109">processing</span> <span m="4185189">by</span>
  <span m="4185399">being</span> <span m="4185729">able</span> <span m="4186029">to</span>
  <span m="4186180">deal</span> <span m="4186479">with</span> <span m="4186660">the</span>
  <span m="4186779">fact</span> <span m="4187140">that</span> <span m="4187350">single</span>
  <span m="4187740">words</span> <span m="4188130">have</span> <span m="4188310">multiple</span>
  <span m="4188760">meanings</span> <span m="4189660">not</span> <span m="4189870">only</span>

  <span m="4191069">in</span> <span m="4191220">other</span> <span m="4191430">languages.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4204230">the</span> <span m="4204410">LSTM</span> <span m="4205130">kind</span>
  <span m="4205430">of</span> <span m="4205550">model</span> <span m="4205970">that</span>
  <span m="4206180">ELMo</span> <span m="4206510">used,</span> <span m="4207380">these</span>
  <span m="4207650">guys</span> <span m="4207950">say,</span> <span m="4208220">well,</span>
  <span m="4208430">let's</span> <span m="4209330">hop</span> <span m="4209660">on</span>
  <span m="4209780">the</span> <span m="4209900">bandwagon,</span> <span m="4210620">use</span>
  <span m="4211130">the</span> <span m="4211700">Transformer-based</span> <span m="4212930">architecture.</span>
  <span m="4214790">And</span> <span m="4215360">then</span> <span m="4215720">they</span>
  <span m="4216320">introduced</span> <span m="4216920">some</span> <span m="4217160">interesting</span>
  <span m="4217730">tricks.</span></p><p><span m="4218570">So</span> <span m="4218780">one</span>
  <span m="4218990">of</span> <span m="4219110">the</span> <span m="4219200">problems</span>
  <span m="4219740">with</span> <span m="4219920">Transformers</span> <span m="4221510">is</span>
  <span m="4221840">if</span> <span m="4222050">you</span> <span m="4222200">stack</span>
  <span m="4222710">them</span> <span m="4222980">on</span> <span m="4223130">top</span>
  <span m="4223460">of</span> <span m="4223610">each</span> <span m="4223820">other</span>
  <span m="4225210">there</span> <span m="4225320">are</span> <span m="4225380">many</span>
  <span m="4225680">paths</span> <span m="4226670">from</span> <span m="4226970">any</span>
  <span m="4227180">of</span> <span m="4227300">the</span> <span m="4227450">inputs</span>
  <span m="4227930">to</span> <span m="4228080">any</span> <span m="4228320">of</span>
  <span m="4228470">the</span> <span m="4228590">intermediate</span> <span m="4229280">nodes</span>
  <span m="4229700">and</span> <span m="4229820">the</span> <span m="4229940">outputs.</span>
  <span m="4231210">And</span> <span m="4231290">so</span> <span m="4231980">if</span>
  <span m="4232190">you're</span> <span m="4232400">doing</span> <span m="4232760">self-attention,</span>
  <span m="4233930">you're</span> <span m="4234140">trying</span> <span m="4234470">to</span>
  <span m="4234620">figure</span> <span m="4235010">out</span> <span m="4235760">where</span>
  <span m="4237290">the</span> <span m="4237500">output</span> <span m="4237980">should</span>
  <span m="4238220">pay</span> <span m="4238520">attention</span> <span m="4239150">to</span>
  <span m="4239390">the</span> <span m="4239570">input,</span> <span m="4241070">the</span>
  <span m="4241280">answer,</span> <span m="4241730">of</span> <span m="4241820">course,</span>
  <span m="4242210">is</span> <span m="4242420">like,</span> <span m="4242720">if</span>
  <span m="4242870">you're</span> <span m="4242990">trying</span> <span m="4243290">to</span>
  <span m="4243410">reconstruct</span> <span m="4244160">the</span> <span m="4244280">input,</span>
  <span m="4245810">if</span> <span m="4246020">the</span> <span m="4246230">input</span>
  <span m="4246950">is</span> <span m="4247550">present</span> <span m="4248330">in</span>
  <span m="4248480">your</span> <span m="4248660">model,</span> <span m="4249590">what</span>
  <span m="4249860">you</span> <span m="4249980">will</span> <span m="4250100">learn</span>
  <span m="4250700">is</span> <span m="4251000">that</span> <span m="4251420">the</span>
  <span m="4251780">corresponding</span> <span m="4252680">word</span> <span m="4253070">is</span>
  <span m="4253250">the</span> <span m="4253370">right</span> <span m="4253670">word</span>
  <span m="4254210">for</span> <span m="4254450">your</span> <span m="4254630">output.</span>
  <span m="4255950">So</span> <span m="4256130">they</span> <span m="4256280">have</span>
  <span m="4256430">to</span> <span m="4256580">prevent</span> <span m="4257030">that</span>
  <span m="4257270">from</span> <span m="4257540">happening.</span> <span m="4258720">And</span>
  <span m="4258770">so</span> <span m="4258980">the</span> <span m="4259100">way</span>
  <span m="4259310">they</span> <span m="4259700">do</span> <span m="4260000">it</span>
  <span m="4260330">is</span> <span m="4260570">by</span> <span m="4260810">masking</span>
  <span m="4261530">off,</span> <span m="4262610">at</span> <span m="4262850">each</span>
  <span m="4263120">level,</span> <span m="4264050">some</span> <span m="4264380">fraction</span>
  <span m="4265310">of</span> <span m="4265550">the</span> <span m="4265670">words</span>
  <span m="4266510">or</span> <span m="4266720">of</span> <span m="4266840">the</span>
  <span m="4267020">inputs</span> <span m="4267590">at</span> <span m="4267770">that</span>
  <span m="4268040">level.</span></p><p><span m="4269460">So</span> <span m="4269600">what</span>
  <span m="4269810">this</span> <span m="4270050">is</span> <span m="4270230">doing</span>
  <span m="4270770">is</span> <span m="4271010">it's</span> <span m="4271220">a</span>
  <span m="4271280">little</span> <span m="4271610">bit</span> <span m="4271880">like</span>
  <span m="4272210">the</span> <span m="4272360">skip-gram</span> <span m="4273020">model</span>
  <span m="4273620">in</span> <span m="4273800">Word2Vec,</span> <span m="4275120">where</span>
  <span m="4275510">it's</span> <span m="4275810">trying</span> <span m="4276140">to</span>
  <span m="4276290">predict</span> <span m="4276860">the</span> <span m="4277010">likelihood</span>
  <span m="4278240">of</span> <span m="4278420">some</span> <span m="4278720">word,</span>
  <span m="4279770">except</span> <span m="4280190">it</span> <span m="4280280">doesn't</span>
  <span m="4280730">know</span> <span m="4281090">what</span> <span m="4281810">a</span>
  <span m="4281870">significant</span> <span m="4282560">fraction</span> <span m="4283100">of</span>
  <span m="4283250">the</span> <span m="4283370">words</span> <span m="4283790">are.</span>
  <span m="4284940">And</span> <span m="4285020">so</span> <span m="4285260">it</span>
  <span m="4285380">can't</span> <span m="4285800">overfit</span> <span m="4287030">in</span>
  <span m="4287180">the</span> <span m="4287270">way</span> <span m="4287480">that</span>
  <span m="4287630">I</span> <span m="4287750">was</span> <span m="4287960">just</span>
  <span m="4288170">suggesting.</span> <span m="4289910">So</span> <span m="4290060">this</span>
  <span m="4290300">turned</span> <span m="4290570">out</span> <span m="4290720">to</span>
  <span m="4290840">be</span> <span m="4291020">a</span> <span m="4291110">good</span>
  <span m="4291290">idea.</span> <span m="4292820">It's</span> <span m="4293270">more</span>
  <span m="4293540">complicated.</span></p><p><span m="4294380">Again,</span> <span
  m="4294740">for</span> <span m="4294980">the</span> <span m="4295130">details,</span>
  <span m="4296190">you</span> <span m="4296270">have</span> <span m="4296420">to</span>
  <span m="4296540">read</span> <span m="4296780">the</span> <span m="4296870">paper.</span>

  <span m="4583190">tokens.</span> <span m="4584180">So</span> <span m="4584420">for</span>
